<div id="page-2173" class="elements-box post-2173 page type-page status-publish hentry">
<h5><span style="color: #339966;">ဖားေအာက္ေတာရဆရာေတာ္ႀကီး ဘဒၵႏၲအာအာစိဏၰ ေဟာၾကားေတာ္မူေသာ တရားေတာ္မ်ား စုစည္းမွု (MP3)</span></h5>
<h5><a href="https://www.thitsarparamisociety.com/paauk-sayadaw-ebook/" target="_blank"><span style="color: #339966;">ဖားေအာက္ေတာရဆရာေတာ္ႀကီး ဘဒၵႏၲအာအာစိဏၰ ေရးသားေတာ္မူေသာ တရားစာအုပ္မ်ား</span></a></h5>
<p><span style="color: #ffcc00;"><a href="https://media.thitsarparamisociety.com/mp3/Pa-Auk/PaAukSayadawGyi-The-only-way-part-to-the-Nibbana-Singapore-2012.mp3" target="_blank"><span style="color: #ffcc00;">နိဗၺာန္သို႔ သြားရာ တစ္ေၾကာင္းတည္းေသာလမ္း</span></a></span></p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<h5><span style="color: #339966;"><strong>အရွင္အာနႏၵာ၏ ဘ၀ဇာတ္ေၾကာင္းမွတ္ေက်ာက္ တရားေတာ္မ်ား</strong></span></h5>
<p><span style="color: #ffcc00;"> <a href="https://media.thitsarparamisociety.com/mp3/Pa-Auk/AshinAnada/AshinAnada-01.mp3"><span style="color: #ffcc00;">၁။ အာနႏၵေတၳရ အပါဒါန္ (၁)</span></a></span></p>
<p><span style="color: #ffcc00;"><a href="https://media.thitsarparamisociety.com/mp3/Pa-Auk/AshinAnada/AshinAnada-02.mp3"><span style="color: #ffcc00;">၂။ အာနႏၵေတၳရ အပါဒါန္ (၂)</span></a></span></p>
<p><span style="color: #ffcc00;"><a href="https://media.thitsarparamisociety.com/mp3/Pa-Auk/AshinAnada/AshinAnada-03.mp3"><span style="color: #ffcc00;">၃။ အာနႏၵေတၳရ အပါဒါန္ (၃)</span></a></span></p>
<p><span style="color: #ffcc00;"><a href="https://media.thitsarparamisociety.com/mp3/Pa-Auk/AshinAnada/AshinAnada-04.mp3"><span style="color: #ffcc00;">၄။ အာနႏၵေတၳရ အပါဒါန္ (၄)</span></a></span></p>
<p><span style="color: #ffcc00;"><a href="https://media.thitsarparamisociety.com/mp3/Pa-Auk/AshinAnada/AshinAnada-05.mp3"><span style="color: #ffcc00;">၅။ အာနႏၵေတၳရ အပါဒါန္ (၅)</span></a></span></p>

<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p><span style="color: #00ffff;">Disk (2)</span></p>
<h5><span style="color: #339966;">၁။စူဠဟတၳိပေဒါပမ သုတၱန္ မဟာဟတၳိ ပေဒါပမ သုတၱန္ </span></h5>

		}; #>

	if ( ! _.isUndefined( data.model.autoplay ) && data.model.autoplay ) {

					}
				#>

					}

					<span>MP3</span>
					<input type="text" disabled="disabled" data-setting="mp3" value="{{ data.model.mp3 }}" />

				</label>
				<# } #>
